      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 

      <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/pere#Middle_English" title="pere">pere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/pere#Old_English" title="pere">pere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/peru" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/peru">*peru</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Latin/pira&action=edit&redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Latin/pira (page does not exist)">*pira</a></i>, originally the plural of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/pirum#Latin" title="pirum">pirum</a></i> but reconstrued as a feminine singular, ultimately a loanword from an unknown Mediterranean <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stratum_(linguistics)" class="extiw" title="w:Stratum (linguistics)">substrate</a></span> source. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href="/wiki/Peere#Saterland_Frisian" title="Peere">Peere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/peer#Dutch" title="peer">peer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A6re#Danish" title="pære">pære</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/poire#French" title="poire">poire</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Birne#German" title="Birne">Birne</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/pera#Icelandic" title="pera">pera</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A4ron#Swedish" title="päron">päron</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">?</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 

      <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pear</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pears#English" title="pears">pears</a></b>) </p> 

      <ol>

       <li>An edible fruit produced by the pear tree, similar to an <a href="/wiki/apple" title="apple">apple</a> but typically elongated towards the stem.</li> 

       <li>A type of fruit tree (<i><a href="/wiki/Pyrus_communis" title="Pyrus communis">Pyrus communis</a></i>). <span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym ▲</a></span>

        <dl>

         <dd>

          <span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pear_tree#English" title="pear tree">pear tree</a></span></span>

         </dd>

        </dl></li> 

       <li>The wood of the pear tree (<a href="/wiki/pearwood" title="pearwood">pearwood</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=pear_wood&action=edit&redlink=1" class="new" title="pear wood (page does not exist)">pear wood</a>).</li> 

       <li><a href="/wiki/choke_pear" title="choke pear">Choke pear</a> (a <a href="/wiki/torture" title="torture">torture</a> device).</li> 

       <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jamaican_English" class="extiw" title="w:Jamaican English">Jamaica</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/avocado" title="avocado">avocado</a>, <a href="/wiki/alligator_pear" title="alligator pear">alligator pear</a></li> 

       <li>A desaturated <a href="/wiki/chartreuse" title="chartreuse">chartreuse</a> yellow <a href="/wiki/colour" title="colour">colour</a>, like that of a pear. 

        <dl>

         <dd>

          <div class="color-panel">

           pear: <span style="background-color:#D1E231; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span>

          </div>

         </dd>

        </dl></li>

      </ol>

       <li>Richard Allsopp, editor, <i>Dictionary of Caribbean English Usage</i>, Kingston, Jamaica: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_the_West_Indies_Press" class="extiw" title="w:University of the West Indies Press">University of the West Indies Press</a>, 1996 (2003 printing), <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9789766401450" title="Special:BookSources/9789766401450">→ISBN</a></small>, page 434</li>

      </ul> 

      <hr> 

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="West_Frisian">West Frisian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=23" title="Edit section: West Frisian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=24" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 

      <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href="/wiki/par#Old_Frisian" title="par">p?r</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/par#Latin" title="par">p?r</a></i>. </p> 

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=25" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 

      <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fy">pear</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fy p-form-of" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/pearen#West_Frisian" title="pearen">pearen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fy diminutive-form-of" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/pearke#West_Frisian" title="pearke">pearke</a></b>) </p> 

      <ol>

       <li><a href="/wiki/pair" title="pair">pair</a>, <a href="/wiki/couple" title="couple">couple</a></li>

      </ol> 

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Further_reading_2">Further reading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&action=edit&section=26" title="Edit section: Further reading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4> 

      <ul>

       <li>“<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gtb.inl.nl/iWDB/search?wdb=WFT&actie=article&id=75119">pear</a>?, in <cite>Wurdboek fan de Fryske taal</cite> (in Dutch), 2011</li>
